    49	    public StreamDescription enableStream(String tableName, String tableArn, String viewType, String region) {
    50	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    51	        StreamDescription existing = streams.get(key);
    52	        if (existing != null && "ENABLED".equals(existing.getStreamStatus())) {
    53	            return existing;
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        Instant now = Instant.now();
    57	        String label = STREAM_LABEL_FORMAT.format(now);
    58	        String streamArn = tableArn + "/stream/" + label;
    59	
    60	        StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
    61	        sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
    62	        sd.setStreamLabel(label);
    63	        sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");
    64	        sd.setStreamViewType(viewType);
    65	        sd.setTableName(tableName);
    66	        sd.setCreationDateTime(now);
    67	        sd.setStartingSequenceNumber(String.format("%021d", 1));
    68	
    69	        streams.put(key, sd);
    70	        records.put(streamArn, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
    71	        LOG.infov("Enabled stream for table {0} in region {1}: {2}", tableName, region, streamArn);
    72	        return sd;
    73	    }

    75	    public void disableStream(String tableName, String region) {
    76	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    77	        StreamDescription sd = streams.get(key);
    78	        if (sd != null) {
    79	            sd.setStreamStatus("DISABLED");

    81	        }

    85	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);

    93	    public void captureEvent(String tableName, String eventName,
    94	                             JsonNode oldItem, JsonNode newItem,
    95	                             TableDefinition table, String region) {
    96	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    97	        StreamDescription sd = streams.get(key);
    98	        if (sd == null || !"ENABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus())) {
    99	            return;
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        long seq = sequenceCounter.incrementAndGet();
   103	        String sequenceNumber = String.format("%021d", seq);
   104	
   105	        JsonNode sourceItem = newItem != null ? newItem : oldItem;
   106	        ObjectNode keys = buildKeys(sourceItem, table);
   107	
   108	        String viewType = sd.getStreamViewType();
   109	        JsonNode newImage = buildImage(newItem, viewType, true);
   110	        JsonNode oldImage = buildImage(oldItem, viewType, false);
   111	
   112	        DynamoDbStreamRecord record = new DynamoDbStreamRecord();
   113	        record.setEventId(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
   114	        record.setEventVersion("1.1");
   115	        record.setEventName(eventName);
   116	        record.setEventSource("aws:dynamodb");
   117	        record.setAwsRegion(region);
   118	        record.setSequenceNumber(sequenceNumber);
   119	        record.setApproximateCreationDateTime(Instant.now().getEpochSecond());
   120	        record.setKeys(keys);
   121	        record.setNewImage(newImage);
   122	        record.setOldImage(oldImage);
   123	        record.setStreamViewType(viewType);
   124	
   125	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(sd.getStreamArn());
   126	        if (deque != null) {
   127	            deque.addLast(record);
   128	            while (deque.size() > MAX_RECORDS) {
   129	                deque.pollFirst();
   130	            }
   131	        }
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    private ObjectNode buildKeys(JsonNode item, TableDefinition table) {
   135	        ObjectNode keys = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   136	        if (item == null) {
   137	            return keys;
   138	        }
   139	        for (KeySchemaElement ks : table.getKeySchema()) {
   140	            String attrName = ks.getAttributeName();
   141	            if (item.has(attrName)) {
   142	                keys.set(attrName, item.get(attrName));
   143	            }
   144	        }
   145	        return keys;
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    private JsonNode buildImage(JsonNode item, String viewType, boolean isNewImage) {
   149	        if (item == null) {
   150	            return null;
   151	        }
   152	        return switch (viewType) {
   153	            case "KEYS_ONLY" -> null;
   154	            case "NEW_IMAGE" -> isNewImage ? item : null;
   155	            case "OLD_IMAGE" -> !isNewImage ? item : null;
   156	            case "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES" -> item;
   157	            default -> null;
   158	        };
   159	    }

   161	    public List<StreamDescription> listStreams(String tableNameFilter, String region) {
   162	        List<StreamDescription> result = new ArrayList<>();
   163	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams.values()) {
   164	            if (tableNameFilter != null && !tableNameFilter.equals(sd.getTableName())) {
   165	                continue;
   166	            }
   167	            if (region != null && !sd.getStreamArn().contains(":" + region + ":")) {
   168	                continue;
   169	            }
   170	            result.add(sd);
   171	        }
   172	        return result;
   173	    }

   175	    public StreamDescription describeStream(String streamArn) {
   176	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams.values()) {
   177	            if (streamArn.equals(sd.getStreamArn())) {
   178	                return sd;
   179	            }
   180	        }
   181	        throw new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   182	                "Stream not found: " + streamArn, 400);
   183	    }
   184	
   185	    public String getShardIterator(String streamArn, String shardId,
   186	                                   String iteratorType, String sequenceNumber) {
   187	        StreamDescription sd = describeStream(streamArn);
   188	        if (!"ENABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus()) && !"DISABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus())) {
   189	            throw new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   190	                    "Stream not found: " + streamArn, 400);
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(streamArn);
   194	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> snapshot = deque != null ? new ArrayList<>(deque) : List.of();
   195	
   196	        int position = switch (iteratorType) {
   197	            case "TRIM_HORIZON" -> 0;
   198	            case "LATEST" -> snapshot.size();
   199	            case "AT_SEQUENCE_NUMBER" -> findSequencePosition(snapshot, sequenceNumber, false);
   200	            case "AFTER_SEQUENCE_NUMBER" -> findSequencePosition(snapshot, sequenceNumber, true);
   201	            default -> throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   202	                    "Unknown iterator type: " + iteratorType, 400);
   203	        };
   204	
   205	        return encodeIterator(streamArn, position);
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    private int findSequencePosition(List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> records, String targetSeq, boolean after) {
   209	        for (int i = 0; i < records.size(); i++) {
   210	            String seq = records.get(i).getSequenceNumber();
   211	            int cmp = seq.compareTo(targetSeq);
   212	            if (after ? cmp > 0 : cmp >= 0) {
   213	                return i;
   214	            }
   215	        }
   216	        return records.size();
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    public record GetRecordsResult(List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> records, String nextShardIterator) {}
   220	
   221	    public GetRecordsResult getRecords(String shardIterator, Integer limit) {
   222	        String[] parts = decodeIterator(shardIterator);
   223	        String streamArn = parts[0];
   224	        int position = Integer.parseInt(parts[1]);
   225	
   226	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(streamArn);
   227	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> snapshot = deque != null ? new ArrayList<>(deque) : List.of();
   228	
   229	        int effectiveLimit = limit != null ? limit : 100;
   230	        int end = Math.min(position + effectiveLimit, snapshot.size());
   231	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> page = snapshot.subList(position, end);
   232	
   233	        String nextIterator = encodeIterator(streamArn, end);
   234	        return new GetRecordsResult(new ArrayList<>(page), nextIterator);
   235	    }
   236	
   237	    private String encodeIterator(String streamArn, int position) {
   238	        String raw = streamArn + "|" + position;
   239	        return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(raw.getBytes());
   240	    }
   241	
   242	    private String[] decodeIterator(String iterator) {
   243	        try {
   244	            String raw = new String(Base64.getDecoder().decode(iterator));
   245	            int lastPipe = raw.lastIndexOf('|');
   246	            if (lastPipe < 0) {
   247	                throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid shard iterator", 400);
   248	            }
   249	            return new String[]{raw.substring(0, lastPipe), raw.substring(lastPipe + 1)};
   250	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
   251	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid shard iterator", 400);
   252	        }
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    private String streamKey(String region, String tableName) {
   256	        return region + "::" + tableName;
   257	    }
   258	}
   259

    78	    private void loadPersistedItems() {
    79	        if (itemStore == null) return;
    80	        for (String key : itemStore.keys()) {
    81	            itemStore.get(key).ifPresent(items ->
    82	                itemsByTable.put(key, new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>(items)));
    83	        }
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    private void persistItems(String storageKey) {
    87	        if (itemStore == null) return;
    88	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
    89	        if (items != null) {
    90	            itemStore.put(storageKey, new HashMap<>(items));
    91	        } else {
    92	            itemStore.delete(storageKey);
    93	        }
    94	    }

   112	    public TableDefinition createTable(String tableName,
   113	                                        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema,
   114	                                        List<AttributeDefinition> attributeDefinitions,
   115	                                        Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity,
   116	                                        List<GlobalSecondaryIndex> gsis, String region) {

   121	    public TableDefinition createTable(String tableName,
   122	                                        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema,
   123	                                        List<AttributeDefinition> attributeDefinitions,
   124	                                        Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity,
   125	                                        List<GlobalSecondaryIndex> gsis,
   126	                                        List<LocalSecondaryIndex> lsis,
   127	                                        String region) {
   128	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   129	        if (tableStore.get(storageKey).isPresent()) {
   130	            throw new AwsException("ResourceInUseException",
   131	                    "Table already exists: " + tableName, 400);
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        TableDefinition table = new TableDefinition(tableName, keySchema, attributeDefinitions,
   135	                region, regionResolver.getAccountId());
   136	        if (readCapacity != null && writeCapacity != null) {
   137	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setReadCapacityUnits(readCapacity);
   138	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setWriteCapacityUnits(writeCapacity);
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        if (gsis != null && !gsis.isEmpty()) {
   142	            for (GlobalSecondaryIndex gsi : gsis) {
   143	                gsi.setIndexArn(table.getTableArn() + "/index/" + gsi.getIndexName());
   144	            }
   145	            table.setGlobalSecondaryIndexes(new ArrayList<>(gsis));
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        if (lsis != null && !lsis.isEmpty()) {
   149	            String tablePk = table.getPartitionKeyName();
   150	            for (LocalSecondaryIndex lsi : lsis) {
   151	                String lsiPk = lsi.getPartitionKeyName();
   152	                if (!tablePk.equals(lsiPk)) {
   153	                    throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   154	                            "LocalSecondaryIndex partition key must match table partition key", 400);
   155	                }
   156	                lsi.setIndexArn(table.getTableArn() + "/index/" + lsi.getIndexName());
   157	            }
   158	            table.setLocalSecondaryIndexes(new ArrayList<>(lsis));
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
   162	        itemsByTable.put(storageKey, new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>());
   163	        LOG.infov("Created table: {0} in region {1}", tableName, region);
   164	        return table;
   165	    }

   172	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);

   188	    public void deleteTable(String tableName, String region) {
   189	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   190	        if (tableStore.get(storageKey).isEmpty()) {
   191	            throw resourceNotFoundException(tableName);
   192	        }
   193	        tableStore.delete(storageKey);
   194	        itemsByTable.remove(storageKey);
   195	        if (itemStore != null) {

   197	        }
   198	        if (streamService != null) {
   199	            streamService.deleteStream(tableName, region);
   200	        }
   201	        LOG.infov("Deleted table: {0}", tableName);
   202	    }

   223	    public void putItem(String tableName, JsonNode item,
   224	                         String conditionExpression,
   225	                         JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues,
   226	                         String region) {
   227	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   228	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   229	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   230	
   231	        String itemKey = buildItemKey(table, item);
   232	        var tableItems = itemsByTable.computeIfAbsent(storageKey, k -> new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>());
   233	
   234	        JsonNode existing = tableItems.get(itemKey);
   235	
   236	        if (conditionExpression != null) {
   237	            evaluateCondition(existing, conditionExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        tableItems.put(itemKey, item);
   241	        persistItems(storageKey);
   242	        LOG.debugv("Put item in {0}: key={1}", tableName, itemKey);
   243	
   244	        if (streamService != null) {
   245	            streamService.captureEvent(tableName,
   246	                    existing == null ? "INSERT" : "MODIFY", existing, item, table, region);
   247	        }
   248	    }

   257	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));

   275	    public JsonNode deleteItem(String tableName, JsonNode key,
   276	                                String conditionExpression,
   277	                                JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues,
   278	                                String region) {
   279	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   280	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   281	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   282	
   283	        String itemKey = buildItemKey(table, key);
   284	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
   285	        if (items == null) return null;
   286	
   287	        if (conditionExpression != null) {
   288	            JsonNode existing = items.get(itemKey);
   289	            evaluateCondition(existing, conditionExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues);
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        JsonNode removed = items.remove(itemKey);
   293	        persistItems(storageKey);
   294	        LOG.debugv("Deleted item from {0}: key={1}", tableName, itemKey);
   295	
   296	        if (streamService != null && removed != null) {
   297	            streamService.captureEvent(tableName, "REMOVE", removed, null, table, region);
   298	        }
   299	
   300	        return removed;
   301	    }

    35	    public Response handle(String action, JsonNode request, String region) throws Exception {
    36	        return switch (action) {
    37	            case "CreateTable" -> handleCreateTable(request, region);
    38	            case "DeleteTable" -> handleDeleteTable(request, region);
    39	            case "DescribeTable" -> handleDescribeTable(request, region);
    40	            case "ListTables" -> handleListTables(request, region);
    41	            case "PutItem" -> handlePutItem(request, region);
    42	            case "GetItem" -> handleGetItem(request, region);
    43	            case "DeleteItem" -> handleDeleteItem(request, region);
    44	            case "UpdateItem" -> handleUpdateItem(request, region);
    45	            case "Query" -> handleQuery(request, region);
    46	            case "Scan" -> handleScan(request, region);
    47	            case "BatchWriteItem" -> handleBatchWriteItem(request, region);
    48	            case "BatchGetItem" -> handleBatchGetItem(request, region);
    49	            case "UpdateTable" -> handleUpdateTable(request, region);
    50	            case "DescribeTimeToLive" -> handleDescribeTimeToLive(request, region);
    51	            case "UpdateTimeToLive" -> handleUpdateTimeToLive(request, region);
    52	            case "TransactWriteItems" -> handleTransactWriteItems(request, region);
    53	            case "TransactGetItems" -> handleTransactGetItems(request, region);
    54	            case "TagResource" -> handleTagResource(request, region);
    55	            case "UntagResource" -> handleUntagResource(request, region);
    56	            case "ListTagsOfResource" -> handleListTagsOfResource(request, region);
    57	            default -> Response.status(400)
    58	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnknownOperationException", "Operation " + action + " is not supported."))
    59	                    .build();
    60	
    61	        };
    62	    }

    64	    private Response handleCreateTable(JsonNode request, String region) {
    65	        String tableName = request.path("TableName").asText();
    66	
    67	        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema = new ArrayList<>();
    68	        request.path("KeySchema").forEach(ks ->
    69	                keySchema.add(new KeySchemaElement(
    70	                        ks.path("AttributeName").asText(),
    71	                        ks.path("KeyType").asText())));
    72	
    73	        List<AttributeDefinition> attrDefs = new ArrayList<>();
    74	        request.path("AttributeDefinitions").forEach(ad ->
    75	                attrDefs.add(new AttributeDefinition(
    76	                        ad.path("AttributeName").asText(),
    77	                        ad.path("AttributeType").asText())));
    78	
    79	        Long readCapacity = null;
    80	        Long writeCapacity = null;
    81	        JsonNode pt = request.path("ProvisionedThroughput");
    82	        if (!pt.isMissingNode()) {
    83	            readCapacity = pt.path("ReadCapacityUnits").asLong(5);
    84	            writeCapacity = pt.path("WriteCapacityUnits").asLong(5);
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        List<GlobalSecondaryIndex> gsis = new ArrayList<>();
    88	        JsonNode gsiArray = request.path("GlobalSecondaryIndexes");
    89	        if (!gsiArray.isMissingNode() && gsiArray.isArray()) {
    90	            for (JsonNode gsiNode : gsiArray) {
    91	                String indexName = gsiNode.path("IndexName").asText();
    92	                List<KeySchemaElement> gsiKeySchema = new ArrayList<>();
    93	                gsiNode.path("KeySchema").forEach(ks ->
    94	                        gsiKeySchema.add(new KeySchemaElement(
    95	                                ks.path("AttributeName").asText(),
    96	                                ks.path("KeyType").asText())));
    97	                String projectionType = gsiNode.path("Projection").path("ProjectionType").asText("ALL");
    98	                GlobalSecondaryIndex gsi = new GlobalSecondaryIndex(indexName, gsiKeySchema, null, projectionType);
    99	                JsonNode gsiPt = gsiNode.path("ProvisionedThroughput");
   100	                if (!gsiPt.isMissingNode()) {
   101	                    gsi.getProvisionedThroughput().setReadCapacityUnits(gsiPt.path("ReadCapacityUnits").asLong(0));
   102	                    gsi.getProvisionedThroughput().setWriteCapacityUnits(gsiPt.path("WriteCapacityUnits").asLong(0));
   103	                }
   104	                gsis.add(gsi);
   105	            }
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        List<LocalSecondaryIndex> lsis = new ArrayList<>();
   109	        JsonNode lsiArray = request.path("LocalSecondaryIndexes");
   110	        if (!lsiArray.isMissingNode() && lsiArray.isArray()) {
   111	            for (JsonNode lsiNode : lsiArray) {
   112	                String indexName = lsiNode.path("IndexName").asText();
   113	                List<KeySchemaElement> lsiKeySchema = new ArrayList<>();
   114	                lsiNode.path("KeySchema").forEach(ks ->
   115	                        lsiKeySchema.add(new KeySchemaElement(
   116	                                ks.path("AttributeName").asText(),
   117	                                ks.path("KeyType").asText())));
   118	                String projectionType = lsiNode.path("Projection").path("ProjectionType").asText("ALL");
   119	                lsis.add(new LocalSecondaryIndex(indexName, lsiKeySchema, null, projectionType));
   120	            }
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        String billingMode = request.has("BillingMode")
   124	                ? request.get("BillingMode").asText() : null;
   125	
   126	        TableDefinition table = dynamoDbService.createTable(tableName, keySchema, attrDefs,
   127	                readCapacity, writeCapacity, gsis, lsis, region);
   128	
   129	        if ("PAY_PER_REQUEST".equals(billingMode)) {
   130	            table.setBillingMode("PAY_PER_REQUEST");
   131	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setReadCapacityUnits(0L);
   132	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setWriteCapacityUnits(0L);
   133	        } else {
   134	            table.setBillingMode("PROVISIONED");
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        // Store tags from CreateTable request
   138	        JsonNode tagsNode = request.path("Tags");
   139	        if (tagsNode.isArray()) {
   140	            for (JsonNode tag : tagsNode) {
   141	                table.getTags().put(tag.path("Key").asText(), tag.path("Value").asText());
   142	            }
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        JsonNode streamSpec = request.path("StreamSpecification");
   146	        if (!streamSpec.isMissingNode() && streamSpec.path("StreamEnabled").asBoolean(false)) {
   147	            String viewType = streamSpec.path("StreamViewType").asText("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
   148	            StreamDescription sd = dynamoDbStreamService.enableStream(
   149	                    tableName, table.getTableArn(), viewType, region);
   150	            table.setStreamEnabled(true);
   151	            table.setStreamArn(sd.getStreamArn());
   152	            table.setStreamViewType(viewType);
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   156	        response.set("TableDescription", tableToNode(table));
   157	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   158	    }

   160	    private Response handleDeleteTable(JsonNode request, String region) {
   161	        String tableName = request.path("TableName").asText();
   162	        TableDefinition table = dynamoDbService.describeTable(tableName, region);
   163	        dynamoDbService.deleteTable(tableName, region);
   164	
   165	        table.setTableStatus("DELETING");
   166	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   167	        response.set("TableDescription", tableToNode(table));
   168	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   169	    }

   190	    private Response handlePutItem(JsonNode request, String region) {
   191	        String tableName = request.path("TableName").asText();
   192	        JsonNode item = request.path("Item");
   193	        String returnValues = request.path("ReturnValues").asText("NONE");
   194	        String conditionExpression = request.has("ConditionExpression")
   195	                ? request.get("ConditionExpression").asText() : null;
   196	        JsonNode exprAttrNames = request.has("ExpressionAttributeNames")
   197	                ? request.get("ExpressionAttributeNames") : null;
   198	        JsonNode exprAttrValues = request.has("ExpressionAttributeValues")
   199	                ? request.get("ExpressionAttributeValues") : null;
   200	
   201	        JsonNode oldItem = null;
   202	        if ("ALL_OLD" .equals(returnValues)) {
   203	            dynamoDbService.describeTable(tableName, region);
   204	            oldItem = dynamoDbService.getItem(tableName, item, region);
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        dynamoDbService.putItem(tableName, item, conditionExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues, region);
   208	
   209	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   210	        if ("ALL_OLD" .equals(returnValues) && oldItem != null) {
   211	            response.set("Attributes", oldItem);
   212	        }
   213	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   214	    }

   223	        if (item != null) {

   225	        }
   226	        return Response.ok(response).build();

   242	
   243	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   244	        if ("ALL_OLD" .equals(returnValues) && oldItem != null) {

   247	        return Response.ok(response).build();

   250	    private Response handleUpdateItem(JsonNode request, String region) {
   251	        String tableName = request.path("TableName").asText();
   252	        JsonNode key = request.path("Key");
   253	        JsonNode attributeUpdates = request.path("AttributeUpdates");
   254	        JsonNode exprAttrNames = request.has("ExpressionAttributeNames")
   255	                ? request.get("ExpressionAttributeNames") : null;
   256	        JsonNode exprAttrValues = request.has("ExpressionAttributeValues")
   257	                ? request.get("ExpressionAttributeValues") : null;
   258	        String updateExpression = request.has("UpdateExpression")
   259	                ? request.get("UpdateExpression").asText() : null;
   260	        String conditionExpression = request.has("ConditionExpression")
   261	                ? request.get("ConditionExpression").asText() : null;
   262	        String returnValues = request.path("ReturnValues").asText("NONE");
   263	
   264	        JsonNode updateData = attributeUpdates.isMissingNode() ? null : attributeUpdates;
   265	
   266	        DynamoDbService.UpdateResult result = dynamoDbService.updateItem(
   267	                tableName, key, updateData, updateExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues,
   268	                returnValues, conditionExpression, region);
   269	
   270	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   271	        if ("ALL_NEW" .equals(returnValues) && result.newItem() != null) {
   272	            response.set("Attributes", result.newItem());
   273	        } else if ("ALL_OLD" .equals(returnValues) && result.oldItem() != null) {
   274	            response.set("Attributes", result.oldItem());
   275	        }
   276	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   277	    }

   279	    private Response handleQuery(JsonNode request, String region) {
   280	        String tableName = request.path("TableName").asText();
   281	        JsonNode keyConditions = request.has("KeyConditions") ? request.get("KeyConditions") : null;
   282	        JsonNode exprAttrValues = request.has("ExpressionAttributeValues")
   283	                ? request.get("ExpressionAttributeValues") : null;
   284	        JsonNode exprAttrNames = request.has("ExpressionAttributeNames")
   285	                ? request.get("ExpressionAttributeNames") : null;
   286	        String keyConditionExpr = request.has("KeyConditionExpression")
   287	                ? request.get("KeyConditionExpression").asText() : null;
   288	        String filterExpr = request.has("FilterExpression")
   289	                ? request.get("FilterExpression").asText() : null;
   290	        Integer limit = request.has("Limit") ? request.get("Limit").asInt() : null;
   291	        Boolean scanIndexForward = request.has("ScanIndexForward")
   292	                ? request.get("ScanIndexForward").asBoolean() : null;
   293	        String indexName = request.has("IndexName") ? request.get("IndexName").asText() : null;
   294	        JsonNode exclusiveStartKey = request.has("ExclusiveStartKey")
   295	                ? request.get("ExclusiveStartKey") : null;
   296	
   297	        DynamoDbService.QueryResult result = dynamoDbService.query(tableName, keyConditions,
   298	                exprAttrValues, keyConditionExpr, filterExpr, limit, scanIndexForward, indexName,
   299	                exclusiveStartKey, exprAttrNames, region);
   300	
   301	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   302	        ArrayNode itemsArray = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   303	        result.items().forEach(itemsArray::add);
   304	        response.set("Items", itemsArray);
   305	        response.put("Count", result.items().size());
   306	        response.put("ScannedCount", result.scannedCount());
   307	        if (result.lastEvaluatedKey() != null) {
   308	            response.set("LastEvaluatedKey", result.lastEvaluatedKey());
   309	        }
   310	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   311	    }

    14	public interface StorageBackend<K, V> {
    15	
    16	    void put(K key, V value);
    17	
    18	    Optional<V> get(K key);
    19	
    20	    void delete(K key);
    21	
    22	    List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter);
    23	
    24	    /** Return all keys in this store. */
    25	    Set<K> keys();
    26	
    27	    /** Persist data to disk if applicable. */
    28	    void flush();
    29	
    30	    /** Load data from disk on startup. */
    31	    void load();
    32	
    33	    /** Clear all data. */
    34	    void clear();
    35	}

    18	 * DynamoDB Streams JSON protocol handler.
    19	 * Handles requests with X-Amz-Target prefix {@code DynamoDBStreams_20120810.}.

    21	@ApplicationScoped

    38	    public Response handle(String action, JsonNode request, String region) {
    39	        return switch (action) {
    40	            case "ListStreams" -> handleListStreams(request, region);
    41	            case "DescribeStream" -> handleDescribeStream(request, region);
    42	            case "GetShardIterator" -> handleGetShardIterator(request, region);
    43	            case "GetRecords" -> handleGetRecords(request, region);
    44	            default -> {
    45	                yield Response.status(400)
    46	                        .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnknownOperationException", "Operation " + action + " is not supported."))
    47	                        .build();
    48	            }
    49	        };
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    private Response handleListStreams(JsonNode request, String region) {
    53	        String tableNameFilter = request.has("TableName") ? request.get("TableName").asText() : null;
    54	
    55	        List<StreamDescription> streams = streamService.listStreams(tableNameFilter, region);
    56	
    57	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    58	        ArrayNode streamList = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
    59	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams) {
    60	            ObjectNode entry = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    61	            entry.put("StreamArn", sd.getStreamArn());
    62	            entry.put("StreamLabel", sd.getStreamLabel());
    63	            entry.put("TableName", sd.getTableName());
    64	            streamList.add(entry);
    65	        }
    66	        response.set("Streams", streamList);
    67	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    private Response handleDescribeStream(JsonNode request, String region) {
    71	        String streamArn = request.path("StreamArn").asText();
    72	        StreamDescription sd = streamService.describeStream(streamArn);
    73	
    74	        // Fetch key schema from the table
    75	        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema = List.of();
    76	        try {
    77	            var table = dynamoDbService.describeTable(sd.getTableName(), region);
    78	            keySchema = table.getKeySchema();
    79	        } catch (Exception ignored) {
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    83	        response.set("StreamDescription", describeStreamToNode(sd, keySchema));
    84	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    private ObjectNode describeStreamToNode(StreamDescription sd, List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema) {
    88	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    89	        node.put("StreamArn", sd.getStreamArn());
    90	        node.put("StreamLabel", sd.getStreamLabel());
    91	        node.put("StreamStatus", sd.getStreamStatus());
    92	        node.put("StreamViewType", sd.getStreamViewType());
    93	        node.put("TableName", sd.getTableName());
    94	        node.put("CreationRequestDateTime", sd.getCreationDateTime().getEpochSecond());
    95	
    96	        ArrayNode keySchemaArray = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
    97	        for (KeySchemaElement ks : keySchema) {
    98	            ObjectNode ksNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    99	            ksNode.put("AttributeName", ks.getAttributeName());
   100	            ksNode.put("KeyType", ks.getKeyType());
   101	            keySchemaArray.add(ksNode);
   102	        }
   103	        node.set("KeySchema", keySchemaArray);
   104	
   105	        ArrayNode shards = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   106	        ObjectNode shard = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   107	        shard.put("ShardId", DynamoDbStreamService.SHARD_ID);
   108	        ObjectNode seqRange = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   109	        seqRange.put("StartingSequenceNumber", sd.getStartingSequenceNumber());
   110	        shard.set("SequenceNumberRange", seqRange);
   111	        shards.add(shard);
   112	        node.set("Shards", shards);
   113	
   114	        node.putNull("LastEvaluatedShardId");
   115	        return node;
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    private Response handleGetShardIterator(JsonNode request, String region) {
   119	        String streamArn = request.path("StreamArn").asText();
   120	        String shardId = request.path("ShardId").asText();
   121	        String iteratorType = request.path("ShardIteratorType").asText();
   122	        String sequenceNumber = request.has("SequenceNumber")
   123	                ? request.get("SequenceNumber").asText() : null;
   124	
   125	        String iterator = streamService.getShardIterator(streamArn, shardId, iteratorType, sequenceNumber);
   126	
   127	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   128	        response.put("ShardIterator", iterator);
   129	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    private Response handleGetRecords(JsonNode request, String region) {
   133	        String shardIterator = request.path("ShardIterator").asText();
   134	        Integer limit = request.has("Limit") ? request.get("Limit").asInt() : null;
   135	
   136	        DynamoDbStreamService.GetRecordsResult result = streamService.getRecords(shardIterator, limit);
   137	
   138	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   139	        ArrayNode recordsArray = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   140	        for (DynamoDbStreamRecord record : result.records()) {
   141	            recordsArray.add(recordToNode(record));
   142	        }
   143	        response.set("Records", recordsArray);
   144	        response.put("NextShardIterator", result.nextShardIterator());
   145	        
   146	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    private ObjectNode recordToNode(DynamoDbStreamRecord record) {
   150	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   151	        node.put("eventID", record.getEventId());
   152	        node.put("eventName", record.getEventName());
   153	        node.put("eventVersion", record.getEventVersion());
   154	        node.put("eventSource", record.getEventSource());
   155	        node.put("awsRegion", record.getAwsRegion());
   156	
   157	        ObjectNode dynamodb = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   158	        dynamodb.put("ApproximateCreationDateTime", record.getApproximateCreationDateTime());
   159	        if (record.getKeys() != null) {
   160	            dynamodb.set("Keys", record.getKeys());
   161	        }
   162	        if (record.getNewImage() != null) {
   163	            dynamodb.set("NewImage", record.getNewImage());
   164	        }
   165	        if (record.getOldImage() != null) {
   166	            dynamodb.set("OldImage", record.getOldImage());
   167	        }
   168	        dynamodb.put("SequenceNumber", record.getSequenceNumber());
   169	        dynamodb.put("SizeBytes", 100);
   170	        dynamodb.put("StreamViewType", record.getStreamViewType());
   171	        node.set("dynamodb", dynamodb);
   172	
   173	        return node;
   174	    }

     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;
     2	
     3	import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
     5	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
     6	import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
     7	import org.jboss.logging.Logger;
     8	
     9	import java.io.IOException;
    10	import java.nio.file.Files;
    11	import java.nio.file.Path;
    12	import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption;
    13	import java.util.Collections;
    14	import java.util.List;
    15	import java.util.Map;
    16	import java.util.Optional;
    17	import java.util.Set;
    18	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    19	import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
    20	import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
    21	import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
    22	import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
    23	import java.util.function.Predicate;
    24	
    25	/**
    26	 * Hybrid storage: in-memory reads with async flush to disk.
    27	 * Writes go to memory immediately, then flushed to disk periodically.
    28	 */
    29	public class HybridStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {
    30	
    31	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(HybridStorage.class);
    32	
    33	    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    34	    private final Path filePath;
    35	    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    36	    private final TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference;
    37	    private final ScheduledExecutorService scheduler;
    38	    private final AtomicBoolean dirty = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    39	
    40	    public HybridStorage(Path filePath, TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference, long flushIntervalMs) {
    41	        this.filePath = filePath;
    42	        this.typeReference = typeReference;
    43	        this.objectMapper = new ObjectMapper();
    44	        this.objectMapper.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
    45	        this.objectMapper.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
    46	        this.objectMapper.enable(SerializationFeature.INDENT_OUTPUT);
    47	
    48	        this.scheduler = Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(r -> {
    49	            Thread t = new Thread(r, "hybrid-storage-flush");
    50	            t.setDaemon(true);
    51	            return t;
    52	        });
    53	        this.scheduler.scheduleAtFixedRate(this::flushIfDirty, flushIntervalMs, flushIntervalMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    @Override
    57	    public void put(K key, V value) {
    58	        store.put(key, value);
    59	        dirty.set(true);
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    @Override
    63	    public Optional<V> get(K key) {
    64	        return Optional.ofNullable(store.get(key));
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    @Override
    68	    public void delete(K key) {
    69	        store.remove(key);
    70	        dirty.set(true);
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    @Override
    74	    public List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter) {
    75	        return store.entrySet().stream()
    76	                .filter(e -> keyFilter.test(e.getKey()))
    77	                .map(Map.Entry::getValue)
    78	                .toList();
    79	    }
    80	
    81	    @Override
    82	    public Set<K> keys() {
    83	        return Collections.unmodifiableSet(store.keySet());
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    @Override
    87	    public void flush() {
    88	        persistToDisk();
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    @Override
    92	    public void load() {
    93	        if (!Files.exists(filePath)) {
    94	            LOG.debugv("No persistent file found at {0}, starting with empty store", filePath);
    95	            return;
    96	        }
    97	        try {
    98	            Map<K, V> data = objectMapper.readValue(filePath.toFile(), typeReference);
    99	            store.clear();
   100	            store.putAll(data);
   101	            LOG.infov("Loaded {0} entries from {1}", store.size(), filePath);
   102	        } catch (IOException e) {
   103	            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to load data from {0}", filePath);
   104	        }
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    @Override
   108	    public void clear() {
   109	        store.clear();
   110	        dirty.set(true);
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    public void shutdown() {
   114	        scheduler.shutdown();
   115	        try {
   116	            if (!scheduler.awaitTermination(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS)) {
   117	                scheduler.shutdownNow();
   118	            }
   119	        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
   120	            scheduler.shutdownNow();
   121	            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
   122	        }
   123	        flush();
   124	    }
   125	
   126	    private void flushIfDirty() {
   127	        if (dirty.compareAndSet(true, false)) {
   128	            persistToDisk();
   129	        }
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    private synchronized void persistToDisk() {
   133	        try {
   134	            Files.createDirectories(filePath.getParent());
   135	            Path tempFile = filePath.resolveSibling(filePath.getFileName() + ".tmp");
   136	            objectMapper.writeValue(tempFile.toFile(), store);
   137	            Files.move(tempFile, filePath, StandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING, StandardCopyOption.ATOMIC_MOVE);
   138	            LOG.debugv("Flushed {0} entries to {1}", store.size(), filePath);
   139	        } catch (IOException e) {
   140	            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to persist data to {0}", filePath);
   141	            dirty.set(true);
   142	        }
   143	    }
   144	}
   145

     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;
     2	
     3	import io.github.hectorvent.floci.config.EmulatorConfig;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
     5	import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
     6	import jakarta.inject.Inject;
     7	import org.jboss.logging.Logger;
     8	
     9	import java.nio.file.Path;
    10	import java.util.ArrayList;
    11	import java.util.List;
    12	import java.util.Map;
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Factory that creates StorageBackend instances based on configuration.
    16	 * Tracks all created backends for lifecycle management.
    17	 */
    18	@ApplicationScoped
    19	public class StorageFactory {
    20	
    21	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(StorageFactory.class);
    22	
    23	    private final EmulatorConfig config;
    24	    private final List<StorageBackend<?, ?>> allBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    25	    private final List<HybridStorage<?, ?>> hybridBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    26	    private final List<WalStorage<?, ?>> walBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    27	
    28	    @Inject
    29	    public StorageFactory(EmulatorConfig config) {
    30	        this.config = config;
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    /**
    34	     * Create a storage backend for the given service.
    35	     *
    36	     * @param serviceName   the service name (ssm, sqs, s3)
    37	     * @param fileName      the JSON file name for persistent storage
    38	     * @param typeReference Jackson type reference for deserialization
    39	     */
    40	    public <K, V> StorageBackend<K, V> create(String serviceName, String fileName,
    41	                                               TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference) {
    42	        String mode = resolveMode(serviceName);
    43	        long flushInterval = resolveFlushInterval(serviceName);
    44	        Path basePath = Path.of(config.storage().persistentPath());
    45	        Path filePath = basePath.resolve(fileName);
    46	
    47	        LOG.infov("Creating {0} storage for service {1} (file: {2})", mode, serviceName, filePath);
    48	
    49	        StorageBackend<K, V> backend = switch (mode) {
    50	            case "memory" -> new InMemoryStorage<>();
    51	            case "persistent" -> new PersistentStorage<>(filePath, typeReference);
    52	            case "hybrid" -> {
    53	                var hybrid = new HybridStorage<>(filePath, typeReference, flushInterval);
    54	                hybridBackends.add(hybrid);
    55	                yield hybrid;
    56	            }
    57	            case "wal" -> {
    58	                Path snapshotPath = basePath.resolve(fileName.replace(".json", "-snapshot.json"));
    59	                Path walFilePath = basePath.resolve(fileName.replace(".json", ".wal"));
    60	                long compactionInterval = config.storage().wal().compactionIntervalMs();
    61	                var wal = new WalStorage<>(snapshotPath, walFilePath, typeReference, compactionInterval);
    62	                walBackends.add(wal);
    63	                yield wal;
    64	            }
    65	            default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unknown storage mode: " + mode);
    66	        };
    67	
    68	        // load because loadAll() may run before the service is initialized
    69	        backend.load();
    70	
    71	        allBackends.add(backend);
    72	        return backend;
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    /** Load all storage backends from disk. */
    76	    public void loadAll() {
    77	        for (StorageBackend<?, ?> backend : allBackends) {
    78	            backend.load();
    79	        }
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    /** Flush all storage backends to disk. */
    83	    public void flushAll() {
    84	        for (StorageBackend<?, ?> backend : allBackends) {
    85	            backend.flush();
    86	        }
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    /** Shutdown all managed backends (stop schedulers, close connections). */
    90	    public void shutdownAll() {
    91	        for (HybridStorage<?, ?> hybrid : hybridBackends) {
    92	            hybrid.shutdown();
    93	        }
    94	        for (WalStorage<?, ?> wal : walBackends) {
    95	            wal.shutdown();
    96	        }
    97	        flushAll();
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    private String resolveMode(String serviceName) {
   101	        String globalMode = config.storage().mode();
   102	        return switch (serviceName) {
   103	            case "ssm" -> config.storage().services().ssm().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   104	            case "sqs" -> config.storage().services().sqs().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   105	            case "s3" -> config.storage().services().s3().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   106	            case "dynamodb" -> config.storage().services().dynamodb().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   107	            case "sns" -> config.storage().services().sns().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   108	            case "lambda" -> config.storage().services().lambda().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   109	            case "cloudwatchlogs" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchlogs().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   110	            case "cloudwatchmetrics" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchmetrics().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   111	            case "secretsmanager" -> config.storage().services().secretsmanager().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   112	            case "opensearch" -> config.storage().services().opensearch().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   113	            default -> globalMode;
   114	        };
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    private long resolveFlushInterval(String serviceName) {
   118	        return switch (serviceName) {
   119	            case "ssm" -> config.storage().services().ssm().flushIntervalMs();
   120	            case "dynamodb" -> config.storage().services().dynamodb().flushIntervalMs();
   121	            case "sns" -> config.storage().services().sns().flushIntervalMs();
   122	            case "lambda" -> config.storage().services().lambda().flushIntervalMs();
   123	            case "cloudwatchlogs" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchlogs().flushIntervalMs();
   124	            case "cloudwatchmetrics" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchmetrics().flushIntervalMs();
   125	            case "secretsmanager" -> config.storage().services().secretsmanager().flushIntervalMs();
   126	            case "opensearch" -> config.storage().services().opensearch().flushIntervalMs();
   127	            default -> 5000L;
   128	        };
   129	    }
   130	}

2026-05-30 06:38:34,039 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-299 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear picture. Here's the issue:

1. When a table is created with `StreamSpecification`, the stream is enabled in `DynamoDbStreamService` (in-memory cache) AND the `streamEnabled`, `streamArn`, and `streamViewType` are saved to the `TableDefinition` which is persisted via `tableStore`.

2. However, when the service restarts, `DynamoDbStreamService` does NOT re-read from the persisted `tableStore` to re-create the in-memory stream entries. The `DynamoDbService` constructor loads tables from disk (via `loadPersistedItems` for items), but doesn't restore the streams.

3. Therefore, after restart, `ListStreams` returns an empty list because the in-memory `streams` map is empty even though tables with stream enabled still exist in persistent storage.

Let me check if there's a `loadPersistedTables` or similar in DynamoDbService:

The constructor is:
```java
public DynamoDbService(StorageFactory storageFactory, RegionResolver regionResolver,
                       DynamoDbStreamService streamService) {
    this(storageFactory.create("dynamodb", "dynamodb-tables.json",
            new TypeReference<Map<String, Map<String, TableDefinition>>>() {}),
         storageFactory.create("dynamodb", "dynamodb-items.json",
            new TypeReference<Map<String, Map<String, JsonNode>>>() {}),
         regionResolver, streamService);
}
```

And then the 4-arg constructor calls `loadPersistedItems()` but doesn't restore streams.

Let me look at the full DynamoDbService constructor chain and see what exactly happens:

The `tableStore` is loaded from `dynamodb-tables.json` by the storage factory via `backend.load()`. But the `DynamoDbService` doesn't iterate through these tables to re-enable streams.

Now let me look at whether there are existing tests for this:

2026-05-30 06:38:38,663 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-299 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear understanding of the problem and the solution. Let me also check how the DynamoDbService's main constructor handles things. The problem is:

1. When a table is created with stream settings, the `DynamoDbJsonHandler.handleCreateTable` calls `dynamoDbStreamService.enableStream(tableName, table.getTableArn(), viewType, region)` and saves `streamEnabled`, `streamArn`, `streamViewType` on the `TableDefinition`.

2. The `TableDefinition` is persisted to disk via `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)`.

3. On restart, `tableStore.load()` loads all tables from disk, but `DynamoDbStreamService` has no mechanism to reconstruct its in-memory map from the persisted tables.

The fix should be: After loading persisted items (or alongside), iterate through the persisted tables and for any that have `streamEnabled = true`, re-enable the stream in `DynamoDbStreamService`.

Let me write a script to reproduce the issue first:

Good. Now let me also check the `enableStream` method to make sure it handles the case where a stream already exists properly:

Looking at `DynamoDbStreamService.enableStream`:

```java
public StreamDescription enableStream(String tableName, String tableArn, String viewType, String region) {
    String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    StreamDescription existing = streams.get(key);
    if (existing != null && "ENABLED".equals(existing.getStreamStatus())) {
        return existing;
    }
    // ... creates new stream
}
```

This is fine - if we call it again on restart for an already enabled stream, it will just create a new stream descriptor. But wait, there's an issue: on restart, we'd lose the original `streamLabel` and `creationDateTime` because it creates fresh ones. 

Let me think about this more carefully. The `TableDefinition` stores:
- `streamArn` - contains the label
- `streamViewType`

But `DynamoDbStreamService.enableStream` always creates a new label and new creation time. This could be a problem if we want to restore the exact same stream state.

However, looking at the PR description again: "DynamoDBStreamService doesn't read from the persisted files to populate its cache, so after restarting floci, the ListStreams endpoint returns an empty list."

The primary goal is that `ListStreams` returns the streams that were enabled. For a faithful restoration, we should also try to preserve the original stream label and creation time.

Let me look at how the streamArn is constructed in the TableDefinition vs in enableStream:

- In `enableStream`: `streamArn = tableArn + "/stream/" + label` where `label = STREAM_LABEL_FORMAT.format(now)`
- In `TableDefinition`, the `streamArn` is stored from the result of `enableStream`

So on restart, we could pass the original streamArn details to reconstruct the stream. But the `enableStream` method doesn't accept an existing streamArn. I have two options:

1. Add a new method to `DynamoDbStreamService` that allows restoring a stream with an existing streamArn (or modify `enableStream` to accept optional existing parameters)
2. Keep it simple: the key thing is that `ListStreams` works. The exact label/creation time changing on restart is a minor issue.

Let me look at this from a practical standpoint - the PR says the issue is that ListStreams returns empty after restart. The simplest fix that solves the core problem is to call `enableStream` which creates the stream with a new label. This is acceptable because the stream data (records) are in-memory only anyway and would be lost on restart. The important thing is that the stream is listed as enabled.

But let me also check if there's a better approach - maybe we should preserve the original information. Let me look at what information the `StreamDescription` stores and what `DescribeStream` returns:

From `DynamoDbStreamsJsonHandler.describeStreamToNode`:
- StreamArn, StreamLabel, StreamStatus, StreamViewType, TableName, CreationRequestDateTime, KeySchema, Shards

The `StreamLabel` and `CreationRequestDateTime` would change on restart if we don't preserve them. Let me add a method to restore a stream properly.

Let me modify the approach slightly - add a `restoreStream` method to `DynamoDbStreamService` that accepts all the fields from a persisted stream, or better yet, modify `enableStream` to check if there's already a stored streamArn in the table and reuse it.

Actually, looking at this more carefully, let me think about the simplest correct solution:

The `tableStore` has the `TableDefinition` with `streamArn` and `streamViewType`. The `streamArn` contains the label: `arn:aws:dynamodb:region:account:table/tableName/stream/label`. We can extract the label from the streamArn and use it to restore the stream.

Let me modify the approach to add a `restoreStream` method to `DynamoDbStreamService`:

    private String extractStreamLabel(String streamArn) {
        // streamArn format: arn:aws:dynamodb:region:account:table/tableName/stream/label
        int streamIdx = streamArn.lastIndexOf("/stream/");
        if (streamIdx >= 0) {
            return streamArn.substring(streamIdx + 8); // skip "/stream/"
        }
        // Fallback: generate a label from current time
        return java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter
                .ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd'"'"'T'"'"'HH:mm:ss.SSS")
                .withZone(java.time.ZoneOffset.UTC)
                .format(java.time.Instant.now());

    76	                                  String region, String streamLabel, Instant creationDateTime) {
    77	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    78	        // Only restore if not already present
    79	        if (streams.containsKey(key)) {
    80	            return;
    81	        }
    82	        String streamArn = tableArn + "/stream/" + streamLabel;
    83	        StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
    84	        sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
    85	        sd.setStreamLabel(streamLabel);
    86	        sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");
    87	        sd.setStreamViewType(viewType);
    88	        sd.setTableName(tableName);
    89	        sd.setCreationDateTime(creationDateTime);
    90	        sd.setStartingSequenceNumber(String.format("%021d", 1));
    91	        streams.put(key, sd);
    92	        records.put(streamArn, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
    93	        LOG.infov("Restored stream for table {0} in region {1}: {2}", tableName, region, streamArn);
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    public void disableStream(String tableName, String region) {
    97	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    98	        StreamDescription sd = streams.get(key);
    99	        if (sd != null) {
   100	            sd.setStreamStatus("DISABLED");
   101	            LOG.infov("Disabled stream for table {0} in region {1}", tableName, region);
   102	        }
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    public void deleteStream(String tableName, String region) {
   106	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
   107	        StreamDescription sd = streams.remove(key);
   108	        if (sd != null) {
   109	            records.remove(sd.getStreamArn());
   110	            LOG.infov("Deleted stream for table {0} in region {1}", tableName, region);
   111	        }
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    public void captureEvent(String tableName, String eventName,
   115	                             JsonNode oldItem, JsonNode newItem,
   116	                             TableDefinition table, String region) {
   117	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
   118	        StreamDescription sd = streams.get(key);
   119	        if (sd == null || !"ENABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus())) {
   120	            return;
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        long seq = sequenceCounter.incrementAndGet();
   124	        String sequenceNumber = String.format("%021d", seq);
   125	
   126	        JsonNode sourceItem = newItem != null ? newItem : oldItem;
   127	        ObjectNode keys = buildKeys(sourceItem, table);
   128	
   129	        String viewType = sd.getStreamViewType();
   130	        JsonNode newImage = buildImage(newItem, viewType, true);
   131	        JsonNode oldImage = buildImage(oldItem, viewType, false);
   132	
   133	        DynamoDbStreamRecord record = new DynamoDbStreamRecord();
   134	        record.setEventId(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
   135	        record.setEventVersion("1.1");
   136	        record.setEventName(eventName);
   137	        record.setEventSource("aws:dynamodb");
   138	        record.setAwsRegion(region);
   139	        record.setSequenceNumber(sequenceNumber);
   140	        record.setApproximateCreationDateTime(Instant.now().getEpochSecond());
   141	        record.setKeys(keys);
   142	        record.setNewImage(newImage);
   143	        record.setOldImage(oldImage);
   144	        record.setStreamViewType(viewType);
   145	
   146	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(sd.getStreamArn());
   147	        if (deque != null) {
   148	            deque.addLast(record);
   149	            while (deque.size() > MAX_RECORDS) {
   150	                deque.pollFirst();
   151	            }
   152	        }
   153	    }
   154	
   155	    private ObjectNode buildKeys(JsonNode item, TableDefinition table) {
   156	        ObjectNode keys = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   157	        if (item == null) {
   158	            return keys;
   159	        }
   160	        for (KeySchemaElement ks : table.getKeySchema()) {
   161	            String attrName = ks.getAttributeName();
   162	            if (item.has(attrName)) {
   163	                keys.set(attrName, item.get(attrName));
   164	            }
   165	        }
   166	        return keys;
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    private JsonNode buildImage(JsonNode item, String viewType, boolean isNewImage) {
   170	        if (item == null) {
   171	            return null;
   172	        }
   173	        return switch (viewType) {
   174	            case "KEYS_ONLY" -> null;
   175	            case "NEW_IMAGE" -> isNewImage ? item : null;
   176	            case "OLD_IMAGE" -> !isNewImage ? item : null;
   177	            case "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES" -> item;
   178	            default -> null;
   179	        };
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    public List<StreamDescription> listStreams(String tableNameFilter, String region) {
   183	        List<StreamDescription> result = new ArrayList<>();
   184	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams.values()) {
   185	            if (tableNameFilter != null && !tableNameFilter.equals(sd.getTableName())) {
   186	                continue;
   187	            }
   188	            if (region != null && !sd.getStreamArn().contains(":" + region + ":")) {
   189	                continue;
   190	            }
   191	            result.add(sd);
   192	        }
   193	        return result;
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    public StreamDescription describeStream(String streamArn) {
   197	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams.values()) {
   198	            if (streamArn.equals(sd.getStreamArn())) {
   199	                return sd;
   200	            }
   201	        }
   202	        throw new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   203	                "Stream not found: " + streamArn, 400);
   204	    }
   205	
   206	    public String getShardIterator(String streamArn, String shardId,
   207	                                   String iteratorType, String sequenceNumber) {
   208	        StreamDescription sd = describeStream(streamArn);
   209	        if (!"ENABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus()) && !"DISABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus())) {
   210	            throw new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   211	                    "Stream not found: " + streamArn, 400);
   212	        }
   213	
   214	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(streamArn);
   215	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> snapshot = deque != null ? new ArrayList<>(deque) : List.of();
   216	
   217	        int position = switch (iteratorType) {
   218	            case "TRIM_HORIZON" -> 0;
   219	            case "LATEST" -> snapshot.size();
   220	            case "AT_SEQUENCE_NUMBER" -> findSequencePosition(snapshot, sequenceNumber, false);
   221	            case "AFTER_SEQUENCE_NUMBER" -> findSequencePosition(snapshot, sequenceNumber, true);
   222	            default -> throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   223	                    "Unknown iterator type: " + iteratorType, 400);
   224	        };
   225	
   226	        return encodeIterator(streamArn, position);
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    private int findSequencePosition(List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> records, String targetSeq, boolean after) {
   230	        for (int i = 0; i < records.size(); i++) {
   231	            String seq = records.get(i).getSequenceNumber();
   232	            int cmp = seq.compareTo(targetSeq);
   233	            if (after ? cmp > 0 : cmp >= 0) {
   234	                return i;
   235	            }
   236	        }
   237	        return records.size();
   238	    }
   239	
   240	    public record GetRecordsResult(List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> records, String nextShardIterator) {}
   241	
   242	    public GetRecordsResult getRecords(String shardIterator, Integer limit) {
   243	        String[] parts = decodeIterator(shardIterator);
   244	        String streamArn = parts[0];
   245	        int position = Integer.parseInt(parts[1]);
   246	
   247	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(streamArn);
   248	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> snapshot = deque != null ? new ArrayList<>(deque) : List.of();
   249	
   250	        int effectiveLimit = limit != null ? limit : 100;
   251	        int end = Math.min(position + effectiveLimit, snapshot.size());
   252	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> page = snapshot.subList(position, end);
   253	
   254	        String nextIterator = encodeIterator(streamArn, end);
   255	        return new GetRecordsResult(new ArrayList<>(page), nextIterator);
   256	    }
   257	
   258	    private String encodeIterator(String streamArn, int position) {
   259	        String raw = streamArn + "|" + position;
   260	        return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(raw.getBytes());
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    private String[] decodeIterator(String iterator) {
   264	        try {
   265	            String raw = new String(Base64.getDecoder().decode(iterator));
   266	            int lastPipe = raw.lastIndexOf('|');
   267	            if (lastPipe < 0) {
   268	                throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid shard iterator", 400);
   269	            }
   270	            return new String[]{raw.substring(0, lastPipe), raw.substring(lastPipe + 1)};
   271	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
   272	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid shard iterator", 400);
   273	        }
   274	    }
   275	
   276	    private String streamKey(String region, String tableName) {
   277	        return region + "::" + tableName;
   278	    }
   279	}

    87	    private void loadPersistedStreams() {
    88	        if (streamService == null) return;
    89	        for (String key : tableStore.keys()) {
    90	            tableStore.get(key).ifPresent(table -> {
    91	                if (table.isStreamEnabled() && table.getStreamArn() != null) {
    92	                    // Extract region from the storage key (format: region::tableName)

    99	                            viewType, region, streamLabel, table.getCreationDateTime());
   100	                    LOG.infov("Restored stream for table {0} in region {1}", table.getTableName(), region);
   101	                }
   102	            });
   103	        }
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    private String extractStreamLabel(String streamArn) {
   107	        // streamArn format: arn:aws:dynamodb:region:account:table/tableName/stream/label
   108	        int streamIdx = streamArn.lastIndexOf("/stream/");
   109	        if (streamIdx >= 0) {
   110	            return streamArn.substring(streamIdx + 8); // skip "/stream/"
   111	        }
   112	        // Fallback: generate a label from current time
   113	        return java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter
   114	                .ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSS")
   115	                .withZone(java.time.ZoneOffset.UTC)
   116	                .format(java.time.Instant.now());
   117	    }

   119	    private String extractRegion(String storageKey) {
   120	        int sep = storageKey.indexOf("::");

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.RegionResolver;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.AttributeDefinition;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.KeySchemaElement;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.StreamDescription;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.TableDefinition;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;

import java.util.List;

public class TestStreamsPersistence {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        ObjectMapper mapper = new ObjectMapper();
        
        // Simulate: create table with stream, persist, then simulate restart
        
        // First "run": create table with stream enabled
        InMemoryStorage<String, TableDefinition> tableStore = new InMemoryStorage<>();
        DynamoDbStreamService streamService = new DynamoDbStreamService(mapper);
        RegionResolver regionResolver = new RegionResolver("us-east-1", "000000000000");
        
        DynamoDbService service1 = new DynamoDbService(tableStore, null, regionResolver, streamService);
        
        // Create table with stream settings
        TableDefinition table = service1.createTable(
            "TestTable",
            List.of(new KeySchemaElement("id", "HASH")),
            List.of(new AttributeDefinition("id", "S")),
            5L, 5L, List.of(), List.of(), "us-east-1"
        );
        
        // Simulate enabling stream (as done in DynamoDbJsonHandler)
        StreamDescription sd = streamService.enableStream(
            "TestTable", table.getTableArn(), "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES", "us-east-1");
        table.setStreamEnabled(true);
        table.setStreamArn(sd.getStreamArn());
        table.setStreamViewType("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
        tableStore.put("us-east-1::TestTable", table);  // update persisted
        
        System.out.println("=== After creating table with stream ===");
        System.out.println("Stream ARN: " + sd.getStreamArn());
        System.out.println("Streams in service: " + streamService.listStreams(null, null).size());
        assert streamService.listStreams(null, null).size() == 1 : "Should have 1 stream";
        
        // Now simulate restart: create new DynamoDbService with same tableStore but new streamService
        DynamoDbStreamService streamService2 = new DynamoDbStreamService(mapper);
        DynamoDbService service2 = new DynamoDbService(tableStore, null, regionResolver, streamService2);
        
        System.out.println("\n=== After restart (new DynamoDbStreamService) ===");
        List<StreamDescription> streams = streamService2.listStreams(null, null);
        System.out.println("Streams in service: " + streams.size());
        
        if (streams.isEmpty()) {
            System.out.println("BUG: Streams not restored after restart!");
            System.exit(1);
        } else {
            System.out.println("SUCCESS: Stream restored!");
            System.out.println("Restored stream ARN: " + streams.get(0).getStreamArn());
            System.out.println("Restored stream status: " + streams.get(0).getStreamStatus());
        }
        
        // Verify describe works too
        StreamDescription restored = streamService2.describeStream(sd.getStreamArn());
        System.out.println("DescribeStream: " + restored.getStreamArn());
        assert restored.getStreamArn().equals(sd.getStreamArn()) : "Stream ARN should match";
        
        System.out.println("\nAll tests passed!");
    }
}

Let me check more carefully...\n\nActually, in `HybridStorage` and `InMemoryStorage`, the `put` method stores the reference directly. And `get` returns the stored reference. But since `table` is the same reference stored in the map, the modifications are visible in the store without needing another `put`. \n\nHowever, for persistent storage, the `put` at line 804 serializes and writes the table. The subsequent modifications to the table object (setting stream fields) happen in memory but are NOT persisted again. This means if the system crashes between `updateTable` and the stream enable, the stream settings won\'t be persisted.\n\nBut wait, this is a pre-existing issue not related to our PR. The PR is specifically about restoring streams on restart.\n\nActually, let me look more carefully at the flow:\n\nIn `DynamoDbJsonHandler.handleUpdateTable`:\n```java\nTableDefinition table = dynamoDbService.updateTable(...);  // persists table\n// ... billing mode ...\nJsonNode streamSpec = request.path("StreamSpecification");\nif (!streamSpec.isMissingNode()) {\n    boolean streamEnabled = streamSpec.path("StreamEnabled").asBoolean(false);\n    if (streamEnabled) {\n        String viewType = streamSpec.path("StreamViewType").asText("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");\n        StreamDescription sd = dynamoDbStreamService.enableStream(\n                tableName, table.getTableArn(), viewType, region);\n        table.setStreamEnabled(true);\n        table.setStreamArn(sd.getStreamArn());\n        table.setStreamViewType(viewType);\n    } else {\n        dynamoDbStreamService.disableStream(tableName, region);\n        table.setStreamEnabled(false);\n    }\n}\n```\n\nAfter this, `table` is modified but not re-persisted! This means if you update a table to enable a stream, the stream will work in memory but won\'t survive a restart. But this is a separate issue from what the PR asks for - the PR focuses on creating tables with streams (CreateTable), where the stream is enabled before the table is first persisted (in `createTable`, `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)` happens before the stream is enabled in `handleCreateTable`).\n\nWait, let me re-read `handleCreateTable`:\n```java\nTableDefinition table = dynamoDbService.createTable(...);  // calls tableStore.put(storageKey, table)\n// ... billing mode ...\nJsonNode streamSpec = request.path("StreamSpecification");\nif (!streamSpec.isMissingNode() && streamSpec.path("StreamEnabled").asBoolean(false)) {\n    String viewType = streamSpec.path("StreamViewType").asText("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");\n    StreamDescription sd = dynamoDbStreamService.enableStream(\n            tableName, table.getTableArn(), viewType, region);\n    table.setStreamEnabled(true);\n    table.setStreamArn(sd.getStreamArn());\n    table.setStreamViewType(viewType);\n}\n```\n\nSame issue - `createTable` already called `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)`, then the handler modifies `table` with stream settings. Since `table` is the same object reference (for in-memory/hybrid storage), it will be in the map correctly but may not be persisted to disk until the next flush.\n\nHowever, for the `HybridStorage`, the `put` marks dirty and the async flush will eventually persist the modified object. The `updateTable` method updates the table in `tableStore` at line 804, but the stream changes are made in `DynamoDbJsonHandler.handleUpdateTable` after calling `updateTable`. Let me check that path more carefully:

1. It calls `dynamoDbService.updateTable(...)` which persists the table changes
2. Then it handles `StreamSpecification` - enabling/disabling stream
3. It sets `table.setStreamEnabled(...)`, `table.setStreamArn(...)`, `table.setStreamViewType(...)` on the returned table object

But wait - does this modified table get persisted again? The `updateTable` already called `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)`. After that, the handler modifies the same table object (which is the same reference in the store if it's in-memory, but not if it's a copy). Let me check more carefully...

Actually, in `HybridStorage` and `InMemoryStorage`, the `put` method stores the reference directly. And `get` returns the stored reference. So when `updateTable` does:
```java
TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey).orElseThrow(...);
// ... modify table ...
tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
```

The `table` is the same object that was in the store. After `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)`, the handler continues to modify `table` (setting stream fields). But since `table` is the same reference stored in the map, the modifications are visible in the store without needing another `put`. 

However, for persistent storage, the `put` at line 804 serializes and writes the table. The subsequent modifications to the table object (setting stream fields) happen in memory but are NOT persisted again. This means if the system crashes between `updateTable` and the stream enable, the stream settings won't be persisted.

But wait, this is a pre-existing issue not related to our PR. The PR is specifically about restoring streams on restart.

Actually, let me look more carefully at the flow:

In `DynamoDbJsonHandler.handleUpdateTable`:
```java
TableDefinition table = dynamoDbService.updateTable(...);  // persists table
// ... billing mode ...
JsonNode streamSpec = request.path("StreamSpecification");
if (!streamSpec.isMissingNode()) {
    boolean streamEnabled = streamSpec.path("StreamEnabled").asBoolean(false);
    if (streamEnabled) {
        String viewType = streamSpec.path("StreamViewType").asText("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
        StreamDescription sd = dynamoDbStreamService.enableStream(
                tableName, table.getTableArn(), viewType, region);
        table.setStreamEnabled(true);
        table.setStreamArn(sd.getStreamArn());
        table.setStreamViewType(viewType);
    } else {
        dynamoDbStreamService.disableStream(tableName, region);
        table.setStreamEnabled(false);
    }
}
```

After this, `table` is modified but not re-persisted! This means if you update a table to enable a stream, the stream will work in memory but won't survive a restart. But this is a separate issue from what the PR asks for - the PR focuses on creating tables with streams (CreateTable), where the stream is enabled before the table is first persisted (in `createTable`, `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)` happens before the stream is enabled in `handleCreateTable`).


However, for the `HybridStorage`, the `put` marks dirty and the async flush will eventually persist the modified object. But if the modifications happen after `put`, they might not be captured by the flush if the flush happens before the modifications.

Actually, for `HybridStorage`:
- `put(key, value)` stores the reference in the ConcurrentHashMap and marks dirty
- The flush serializes the current state of the map

So if the handler modifies the table object after `put`, those modifications will be included in the next flush because the same object reference is in the map. The flush serializes the current state, which includes the stream fields. 

But for `PersistentStorage`:
- `put(key, value)` immediately writes to disk
- Subsequent modifications to the value object won't be persisted
