But this is a pre-existing issue that's not directly related to this PR. The PR focuses on restoring streams from persisted tables on startup. Our fix addresses that.

However, I should also fix the UpdateTable persistence issue to be thorough. Let me add a method to persist the table after stream changes:

Actually, let me look at this from a different angle. The `DynamoDbService` should be responsible for persisting stream state changes. Maybe I should add a method like `enableTableStream` and `disableTableStream` to `DynamoDbService` that both update the stream service and persist the table.

But that might be too large a change. Let me focus on the minimal fix for the PR: restoring streams on restart.

Let me also think about another edge case: what if someone uses `PersistentStorage` mode and creates a table with a stream? The flow is:

1. `DynamoDbService.createTable` → `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)` → immediately serializes to disk
2. Back in `handleCreateTable`, stream is enabled: `table.setStreamEnabled(true)`, `table.setStreamArn(...)`, `table.setStreamViewType(...)` 
3. These modifications are NOT persisted because `put` was already called

So with `PersistentStorage`, after restart, the table would be loaded but without stream fields. Our `loadPersistedStreams` would check `table.isStreamEnabled()` which would be false, so it wouldn't restore the stream. This is a problem!

To fix this properly, I need to ensure that stream changes are persisted. The best approach is to re-persist the table after stream changes. Let me modify `DynamoDbJsonHandler` to re-persist the table after stream modifications.

But `DynamoDbJsonHandler` doesn't have access to the table store directly. The cleanest approach would be to add a method to `DynamoDbService` like `saveTable(TableDefinition)` or `updateTableStreamSettings(...)`. 

Let me add a simple `persistTable` method or just re-use the existing update pattern. Actually, the simplest approach: add a `saveTable` method to `DynamoDbService` that puts the table back in the store, and call it from `DynamoDbJsonHandler` after stream changes.

But wait - for `HybridStorage`, the object reference is shared, so changes are automatically reflected. The issue is only with `PersistentStorage` which writes immediately. And for production use, the default is `memory`. But still, let me fix it properly.

Let me add a `persistTable` method to `DynamoDbService` and call it from the handler after modifying stream settings.

Actually, looking again at `DynamoDbService.updateTable`, it calls `tableStore.put(storageKey, table)`. For `HybridStorage`, `put` just does `store.put(key, value)` and marks dirty. Since the value is the same reference, later modifications to the table will be flushed eventually. So for `HybridStorage`, it works correctly.

For `PersistentStorage`, `put` immediately serializes. So the stream settings set after `put` are lost. But `PersistentStorage` is a less common mode.

For `InMemoryStorage`, `put` just stores the reference, so it works.

I think the safest fix is to ensure the table is re-persisted after stream changes in `handleCreateTable` and `handleUpdateTable`. Let me add a method to `DynamoDbService` for this.

Let me add a `persistTable` method and then update the handler to call it:

3. **What about the `streamLabel` extraction?** The `streamArn` format is `arn:aws:dynamodb:region:account:table/tableName/stream/label`. The `extractStreamLabel` method finds the last `/stream/` and extracts the label after it. This should work correctly.

    67	    DynamoDbService(StorageBackend<String, TableDefinition> tableStore,
    68	                    StorageBackend<String, Map<String, JsonNode>> itemStore,
    69	                    RegionResolver regionResolver,
    70	                    DynamoDbStreamService streamService) {
    71	        this.tableStore = tableStore;
    72	        this.itemStore = itemStore;
    73	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    74	        this.streamService = streamService;
    75	        loadPersistedItems();
    76	        loadPersistedStreams();
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    private void loadPersistedItems() {
    80	        if (itemStore == null) return;
    81	        for (String key : itemStore.keys()) {
    82	            itemStore.get(key).ifPresent(items ->
    83	                itemsByTable.put(key, new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>(items)));
    84	        }
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    private void loadPersistedStreams() {
    88	        if (streamService == null) return;
    89	        for (String key : tableStore.keys()) {
    90	            tableStore.get(key).ifPresent(table -> {
    91	                if (table.isStreamEnabled() && table.getStreamArn() != null) {
    92	                    // Extract region from the storage key (format: region::tableName)
    93	                    String region = extractRegion(key);
    94	                    String viewType = table.getStreamViewType() != null
    95	                            ? table.getStreamViewType() : "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES";
    96	                    // Extract stream label from the stored stream ARN
    97	                    String streamLabel = extractStreamLabel(table.getStreamArn());
    98	                    streamService.restoreStream(table.getTableName(), table.getTableArn(),
    99	                            viewType, region, streamLabel, table.getCreationDateTime());
   100	                    LOG.infov("Restored stream for table {0} in region {1}", table.getTableName(), region);
   101	                }
   102	            });
   103	        }
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    private String extractStreamLabel(String streamArn) {
   107	        // streamArn format: arn:aws:dynamodb:region:account:table/tableName/stream/label
   108	        int streamIdx = streamArn.lastIndexOf("/stream/");
   109	        if (streamIdx >= 0) {
   110	            return streamArn.substring(streamIdx + 8); // skip "/stream/"
   111	        }
   112	        // Fallback: generate a label from current time
   113	        return java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter
   114	                .ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSS")
   115	                .withZone(java.time.ZoneOffset.UTC)
   116	                .format(java.time.Instant.now());
   117	    }
   118	
   119	    private String extractRegion(String storageKey) {
   120	        int sep = storageKey.indexOf("::");
   121	        return sep > 0 ? storageKey.substring(0, sep) : "us-east-1";
   122	    }
   123	
   124	    /**
   125	     * Persist a table definition to the store. Called after stream settings
   126	     * are modified to ensure they survive restarts with persistent storage.
   127	     */
   128	    public void persistTable(TableDefinition table, String region) {
   129	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, table.getTableName());
   130	        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
   131	    }

+    private void loadPersistedStreams() {
+        if (streamService == null) return;
+        for (String key : tableStore.keys()) {
+            tableStore.get(key).ifPresent(table -> {
+                if (table.isStreamEnabled() && table.getStreamArn() != null) {
+                    // Extract region from the storage key (format: region::tableName)
+                    String region = extractRegion(key);
+                    String viewType = table.getStreamViewType() != null
+                            ? table.getStreamViewType() : "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES";
+                    // Extract stream label from the stored stream ARN
+                    String streamLabel = extractStreamLabel(table.getStreamArn());
+                    streamService.restoreStream(table.getTableName(), table.getTableArn(),
+                            viewType, region, streamLabel, table.getCreationDateTime());
+                    LOG.infov("Restored stream for table {0} in region {1}", table.getTableName(), region);
+                }
+            });
+        }
+    }
+
+    private String extractStreamLabel(String streamArn) {
+        // streamArn format: arn:aws:dynamodb:region:account:table/tableName/stream/label
+        int streamIdx = streamArn.lastIndexOf("/stream/");
+        if (streamIdx >= 0) {
+            return streamArn.substring(streamIdx + 8); // skip "/stream/"
+        }
+        // Fallback: generate a label from current time
+        return java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter
+                .ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSS")
+                .withZone(java.time.ZoneOffset.UTC)
+                .format(java.time.Instant.now());
+    }
+
+    private String extractRegion(String storageKey) {
+        int sep = storageKey.indexOf("::");
+        return sep > 0 ? storageKey.substring(0, sep) : "us-east-1";
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * Persist a table definition to the store. Called after stream settings
+     * are modified to ensure they survive restarts with persistent storage.
+     */
+    public void persistTable(TableDefinition table, String region) {
+        String storageKey = regionKey(region, table.getTableName());
+        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
+    }
+

+    public void restoreStream(String tableName, String tableArn, String viewType,
+                                  String region, String streamLabel, Instant creationDateTime) {
+        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
+        // Only restore if not already present
+        if (streams.containsKey(key)) {
+            return;
+        }
+        String streamArn = tableArn + "/stream/" + streamLabel;
+        StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
+        sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
+        sd.setStreamLabel(streamLabel);
+        sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");
+        sd.setStreamViewType(viewType);
+        sd.setTableName(tableName);
+        sd.setCreationDateTime(creationDateTime);
+        sd.setStartingSequenceNumber(String.format("%021d", 1));
+        streams.put(key, sd);
+        records.put(streamArn, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
+        LOG.infov("Restored stream for table {0} in region {1}: {2}", tableName, region, streamArn);
+    }

+    private void loadPersistedStreams() {
+        if (streamService == null) return;
+        for (String key : tableStore.keys()) {
+            tableStore.get(key).ifPresent(table -> {
+                if (table.isStreamEnabled() && table.getStreamArn() != null) {
+                    // Extract region from the storage key (format: region::tableName)
+                    String region = extractRegion(key);
+                    String viewType = table.getStreamViewType() != null
+                            ? table.getStreamViewType() : "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES";
+                    // Extract stream label from the stored stream ARN
+                    String streamLabel = extractStreamLabel(table.getStreamArn());
+                    streamService.restoreStream(table.getTableName(), table.getTableArn(),
+                            viewType, region, streamLabel, table.getCreationDateTime());
+                    LOG.infov("Restored stream for table {0} in region {1}", table.getTableName(), region);
+                }
+            });
+        }
+    }
+
+    private String extractStreamLabel(String streamArn) {
+        // streamArn format: arn:aws:dynamodb:region:account:table/tableName/stream/label
+        int streamIdx = streamArn.lastIndexOf("/stream/");
+        if (streamIdx >= 0) {
+            return streamArn.substring(streamIdx + 8); // skip "/stream/"
+        }
+        // Fallback: generate a label from current time
+        return java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter
+                .ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSS")
+                .withZone(java.time.ZoneOffset.UTC)
+                .format(java.time.Instant.now());
+    }
+
+    private String extractRegion(String storageKey) {
+        int sep = storageKey.indexOf("::");
+        return sep > 0 ? storageKey.substring(0, sep) : "us-east-1";
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * Persist a table definition to the store. Called after stream settings
+     * are modified to ensure they survive restarts with persistent storage.
+     */
+    public void persistTable(TableDefinition table, String region) {
+        String storageKey = regionKey(region, table.getTableName());
+        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
+    }
+
     private void persistItems(String storageKey) {
         if (itemStore == null) return;
         var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
diff --git a/src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/services/dynamodb/DynamoDbStreamService.java b/src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/services/dynamodb/DynamoDbStreamService.java

@@ -72,6 +72,27 @@ public class DynamoDbStreamService {
         return sd;
     }
 
+    public void restoreStream(String tableName, String tableArn, String viewType,
+                                  String region, String streamLabel, Instant creationDateTime) {
+        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
+        // Only restore if not already present
+        if (streams.containsKey(key)) {
+            return;
+        }
+        String streamArn = tableArn + "/stream/" + streamLabel;
+        StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
+        sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
+        sd.setStreamLabel(streamLabel);
+        sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");
+        sd.setStreamViewType(viewType);
+        sd.setTableName(tableName);
+        sd.setCreationDateTime(creationDateTime);
+        sd.setStartingSequenceNumber(String.format("%021d", 1));
+        streams.put(key, sd);
+        records.put(streamArn, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
+        LOG.infov("Restored stream for table {0} in region {1}: {2}", tableName, region, streamArn);
+    }
+
     public void disableStream(String tableName, String region) {
         String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
         StreamDescription sd = streams.get(key);
